{\em \mbox{\hyperlink{class_bio_lib_1_1_bio_image}{Bio\+Image}}} & The \mbox{\hyperlink{class_bio_lib_1_1_bio_image}{Bio\+Image}} parameter represents an image object that contains multiple channels and time points. It has a property called Buffers, which is a 3D array that stores the pixel values of the image. The Coords property is a 3D array that stores the coordinates of each pixel in the image\\
\hline
{\em Channel} & The \char`\"{}\+Channel\char`\"{} parameter represents the specific channel of the \mbox{\hyperlink{class_bio_lib_1_1_bio_image}{Bio\+Image}} that you want to analyze. It is used to access the corresponding buffer in the \mbox{\hyperlink{class_bio_lib_1_1_bio_image}{Bio\+Image}}\textquotesingle{}s \char`\"{}\+Buffers\char`\"{} array.\\
\hline
{\em Time} & The \char`\"{}\+Time\char`\"{} parameter represents the time point or frame number in a time-\/lapse sequence.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

The method is returning the index of the buffer with the highest focus quality in the given \mbox{\hyperlink{class_bio_lib_1_1_bio_image}{Bio\+Image}}.

The function \char`\"{}\+Open\+File\char`\"{} opens a bioimage file and returns a \mbox{\hyperlink{class_bio_lib_1_1_bio_image}{Bio\+Image}} object, with options to specify the series, whether to open in a new tab, and whether to add the image to a collection.  


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}

\hline
{\em series} & The \char`\"{}series\char`\"{} parameter is an integer that represents the series number of the image file to be opened. It is used to specify which series of images to open if the file contains multiple series.\\
\hline
{\em tab} & The \char`\"{}tab\char`\"{} parameter is a boolean value that determines whether the file should be opened in a new tab or not. If set to true, the file will be opened in a new tab; if set to false, the file will be opened in the current tab.\\
\hline
{\em add\+To\+Images} & The \char`\"{}add\+To\+Images\char`\"{} parameter is a boolean value that determines whether the opened \mbox{\hyperlink{class_bio_lib_1_1_bio_image}{Bio\+Image}} should be added to a collection of images. If set to true, the \mbox{\hyperlink{class_bio_lib_1_1_bio_image}{Bio\+Image}} will be added to the collection. If set to false, the \mbox{\hyperlink{class_bio_lib_1_1_bio_image}{Bio\+Image}} will not be added to the collection.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The method is returning a \mbox{\hyperlink{class_bio_lib_1_1_bio_image}{Bio\+Image}} object.

{\em file} & The file path of the bioimage to be opened.\\

\hline
{\em tileX} & The {\ttfamily tileX} parameter is an integer that represents the X-\/coordinate of the top-\/left corner of the tile to be opened in the image.\\
\hline
{\em tileY} & The parameter \char`\"{}tile\+Y\char`\"{} is used to specify the starting Y coordinate of the tile when opening a tiled image. It determines the position of the tile within the image.\\
\hline
{\em tile\+SizeX} & The tile\+SizeX parameter is the width of each tile in pixels when opening a tiled image.\\
\hline
{\em tile\+SizeY} & The parameter \char`\"{}tile\+Size\+Y\char`\"{} is the height of each tile in pixels when the image is tiled. It determines the size of the individual tiles that the image is divided into for efficient loading and processing.\\
\hline

{\footnotesize\ttfamily static \mbox{\hyperlink{class_bio_lib_1_1_bio_image}{Bio\+Image}} Bio\+Lib.\+Bio\+Image.\+Substack (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_bio_lib_1_1_bio_image}{Bio\+Image}}}]{orig,  }\item[{int}]{ser,  }\item[{int}]{zs,  }\item[{int}]{ze,  }\item[{int}]{cs,  }\item[{int}]{ce,  }\item[{int}]{ts,  }\item[{int}]{te }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}



The Substack function takes a \mbox{\hyperlink{class_bio_lib_1_1_bio_image}{Bio\+Image}} object and extracts a substack of images based on specified parameters, including series, z-\/slices, channels, and timepoints.  


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em \mbox{\hyperlink{class_bio_lib_1_1_bio_image}{Bio\+Image}}} & The \mbox{\hyperlink{class_bio_lib_1_1_bio_image}{Bio\+Image}} object that represents the original image.\\
\hline
{\em ser} & The parameter \char`\"{}ser\char`\"{} stands for series, which represents the series number of the image stack.\\
\hline
{\em zs} & The parameter \char`\"{}zs\char`\"{} represents the starting z-\/index of the substack. It determines the first z-\/slice to be included in the substack.\\
\hline
{\em ze} & ze is the ending z-\/index of the substack. It represents the last z-\/slice that will be included in the substack.\\
\hline
{\em cs} & The parameter \char`\"{}cs\char`\"{} represents the starting channel index. It indicates the index of the first channel to be included in the substack.\\
\hline
{\em ce} & The parameter \char`\"{}ce\char`\"{} represents the ending channel index. It is used to specify the last channel to include in the substack operation.\\
\hline
{\em ts} & The parameter \char`\"{}ts\char`\"{} stands for \char`\"{}start time point\char`\"{}. It represents the starting time point of the substack in the original \mbox{\hyperlink{class_bio_lib_1_1_bio_image}{Bio\+Image}}.\\
\hline
{\em te} & The parameter \char`\"{}te\char`\"{} represents the end time point of the substack. It is used to specify the last time point to include in the substack.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The method is returning a \mbox{\hyperlink{class_bio_lib_1_1_bio_image}{Bio\+Image}} object. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
